### Open up the Political thingi ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.0"}
	title = stagpal.0.t
	desc = stagpal.0.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Lets get this done
		name = stagpal.0.a
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

### Sopke with deer nobles ###

	id = stagpal.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.1"}
	title = stagpal.1.t
	desc = stagpal.1.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = stagpal.1.a
		add_political_power = 65
		add_stability = -0.08
	}
	option = { # be a nice duke
		name = stagpal.1.b
		add_political_power = -35
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

### Propaganda ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.4"}
	title = stagpal.4.t
	desc = stagpal.4.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #some
		name = stagpal.4.a
		add_political_power = -15
		add_timed_idea = {
  			idea = SPL_Propaganda_for_the_duke
  			days = 14
		}
	}
	option = { #more
		name = stagpal.4.b
		add_political_power = -35
		add_timed_idea = {
  			idea = SPL_Propaganda_for_the_duke
  			days = 35
		}
	}
	option = { #all
		name = stagpal.4.c
		add_political_power = -55
		add_timed_idea = {
  			idea = SPL_Propaganda_for_the_duke
  			days = 70
		}
	}
}

### Improving a shithole ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.5"}
	title = stagpal.5.t
	desc = stagpal.5.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #great
		name = stagpal.5.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		add_manpower = 6000
	}
}

### An almost fatal incident  ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.7"}
	title = stagpal.7.t
	desc = stagpal.7.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #sad duke is sad
		name = stagpal.7.a
		add_political_power = -10
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Duke_is_sad
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id =stagpal.8 days = 90 random = 2160 }#days to hours apllied 90 2160
		}
	}
}

### Duke has new resolves  ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.8"}
	title = stagpal.8.t
	desc = stagpal.8.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #drag Stagpal to the future
		name = stagpal.8.a
		remove_ideas = {
			SPL_Duke_is_sad
		}
		set_country_flag = SPL_Duke_has_overcome_sadness
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPL_political_path_is_now_open
	}
}

### The Declarations of an Oligarchy   ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.9"}
	title = stagpal.9.t
	desc = stagpal.9.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #hold the fuck 
		name = stagpal.9.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SPL_Oligarchy
	}
}

### Deal with anti llama deers   ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.13"}
	title = stagpal.13.t
	desc = stagpal.13.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Heavy Support Campaing for LLamas
		name = stagpal.13.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = {
    		ideology = neutrality
    		popularity = -0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Normal Campaign for llamas
		name = stagpal.13.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
    		ideology = neutrality
    		popularity = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # A small Campaing for LLamas
		name = stagpal.13.c
		add_political_power = -10
		add_stability = 0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 3
			}
		}
	}
}


### School system   ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.14
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.14"}
	title = stagpal.14.t
	desc = stagpal.14.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Seperated, but give both love
		name = stagpal.14.a
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = 0.01
		decrease_illiteracy = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Mix Classes
		name = stagpal.14.b
		add_political_power = -60
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		decrease_illiteracy = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 1
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Seperated, but good llamas can go to deers
		name = stagpal.14.c
		add_political_power = -5
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		decrease_illiteracy = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 1
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

### The First Council Meetin: Second Day: The Choice of Parlament Präsident ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.18
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.18"}
	title = stagpal.18.t
	desc = stagpal.18.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Favour  OLD Deer
		name = stagpal.18.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Praesident_old_Deer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 1
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.19 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { #  Favour Old Llama
		name = stagpal.18.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Praesident_old_Llama
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 2
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.19 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # Favour  new Deer
		name = stagpal.18.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Praesident_new_Deer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 2
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.19 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { #  Favour new Llama
		name = stagpal.18.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Praesident_new_Llama
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 1
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.19 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
}

### The First Council Meetin: forth Day: Old LLama Land ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.20
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.20"}
	title = stagpal.20.t
	desc = stagpal.20.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Old / Old : Deer gets to keep most land
		name = stagpal.20.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 2
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # Old / OLD : LLamas gets back almost everything 
		name = stagpal.20.b
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 3
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # OLD / NEW : a 60% split in gavou dor the Deers
		name = stagpal.20.c
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 1
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # Old / NEW : 50 % each
		name = stagpal.20.e
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {		
			IF = {
				LIMIT = {
					check_variable = { 
						deer_power > llamas_power 
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
    				var = llamas_power
    				value = 1
				}	
				ELSE_IF = {
					LIMIT = {
						check_variable = { 
							deer_power < llamas_power 
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = {
    					var = deer_power
    					value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # OLD / NEW : 60% in favour for llamas
		name = stagpal.20.f
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 1
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # NEW / Old : Deer gets to keep all
		name = stagpal.20.g
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 4
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # NEW / Old : LLamas gain back everything
		name = stagpal.20.h
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 4
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # NEW / NEW : Deer gets to keep almost everything
		name = stagpal.20.i
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 3
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # NEW / NEW : LLamas get many things back
		name = stagpal.20.j
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 2
			}		
			country_event = { id = stagpal.21 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
}

### The First Council Meetin: fifth Day: the nathional Anthem Question ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.21
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.21"}
	title = stagpal.21.t
	desc = stagpal.21.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Go with a new Theme
		name = stagpal.21.a

country_event = {

	title = stagpal.25.t
	desc = stagpal.25.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

		name = stagpal.25.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = llamas_power
    			value = 2
			}	
			country_event = { id =stagpal.26 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # Balance
		name = stagpal.25.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -15
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				LIMIT = {
					check_variable = { 
						deer_power > llamas_power 
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
    				var = llamas_power
    				value = 1
				}	
				ELSE_IF = {
					LIMIT = {
						check_variable = { 
							deer_power < llamas_power 
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = {
    					var = deer_power
    					value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = stagpal.26 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
	option = { # To only small pushes for new live
		name = stagpal.25.b
		add_political_power = 15
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
    			var = deer_power
    			value = 2
			}	
			country_event = { id = stagpal.26 days = 10 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
}

### Councils Fate  ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.31
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.31"}
	title = stagpal.31.t
	desc = stagpal.31.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #To Do // Second Option should not be viewed / but to lazy to do the math now //
		name = stagpal.31.a
		trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { llamas_power_plus_1 = llamas_power }
			add_to_temp_variable = { llamas_power_plus_1 = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { deer_power_plus_1 = deer_power }
            add_to_temp_variable = { deer_power_plus_1 = 1 }
            NOT = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { 
                		deer_power > llamas_power_plus_1
					}			
            		check_variable = { 
                		llamas_power > deer_power_plus_1 
					}
				}
			}		
		}
		country_event = { id = stagpal_oligarchie.0 days =  2 }#days to hours 
		load_focus_tree = { 
			tree = Stagpal_Oligarchy_tree 
			keep_completed = yes 
		}
	}
	option = { #To Do // Second Option should not be viewed / but to lazy to do the math now //
		name = stagpal.31.b
		Trigger  = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { 
					deer_power > llamas_power_plus_1
				}			
				check_variable = { 
					llamas_power > deer_power_plus_1 
				}
			}	
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPL_THE_LLAMAS_ARE_REVOLTING
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SPL_CHAOS_In_the_streats
			days = 35
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = stagpal.76 days = 35 }#days to hours 
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

		hidden_effect = {

				var = Spl_neveu_Wil #Willpower
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Cha #Charisma
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Int #Inteligenz
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Fre #Rasicm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Mor #Morality
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Mac #Power
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Spl_neveu_Rel #Religion
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}

### Rule of rulership   ###
country_event = {
	id = stagpal.57
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.57"}
	title = stagpal.57.t
	desc = stagpal.57.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Harsh and with a steady Fist
		name = stagpal.57.a 
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Mac > 2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_power_overwhelming
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Mac < -2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_power_stinks
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_power_meh
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Harsh but Fair
		name = stagpal.57.b
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Cha > 2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_Charmeur_overkill
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Cha < -2
				}
			}	
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_Charmeur_bad
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_Charmeur_oompa_loompa
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Fair as you can be
		name = stagpal.57.c
		IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Mor > 2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_fairness_saint
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			LIMIT = {
				check_variable = {
					Spl_neveu_Mor < -2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_fairness_what
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			add_political_power = -25
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_fairness_fair
			}
		}
	}
}

	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = stagpal.79.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_DEERS_SLAVE
			add_idea = SPL_DEERS_SLAVE_gone
		}
		save_current_manpower = yes
		1103 = {
			remove_building = {
    			type = industrial_complex
   				level = 1
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Ai_LA_bewohner = state_population }
			multiply_temp_variable = { Ai_LA_bewohner = -0.2 }
			add_manpower = var:Ai_LA_bewohner
		}
		restore_previous_manpower = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = stagpal.88
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.88"}
	title = stagpal.88.t
	desc = stagpal.88.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # What has work will work
		name = stagpal.88.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_BRAINDEAD_Military
			add_idea = SPL_forgeign_military_tactics
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = "AI_LA_Army_Spawn"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_technology = { pre_gw_artillery = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_support = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_engineers = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_mountaineers = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_recon = 1 }
			division_template = {
				name = "LLamas of the Revolution"
				#division_names_group = 
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Protectors of the Mountains"
				#division_names_group = 
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 1\" division_template = \"LLamas of the Revolution\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"

					division = "name = \"Boy 2\" division_template = \"LLamas of the Revolution\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 3\" division_template = \"LLamas of the Revolution\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 4\" division_template = \"LLamas of the Revolution\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 5\" division_template = \"Protectors of the Mountains\" start_experience_factor = 0.75 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 6\" division_template = \"Protectors of the Mountains\" start_experience_factor = 0.75 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}

country_event = {
	id = stagpal.89
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.89"}

	desc = stagpal.89.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Ready for the Future
		name = stagpal.89.a	
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_BRAINDEAD_Military
			add_idea = SPL_selflearned_military_tacticst
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = "AI_LA_Army_Spawn"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_technology = { pre_gw_artillery = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_support = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_engineers = 1 }
			set_technology = { tech_mountaineers = 1 }
			set_technology = { gwtank = 1 }
			set_technology = { motorised_infantry = 1 }
			division_template = {
				name = "Command Group"
				#division_names_group = 
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					mountaineers = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Motorized Support Unit"
				#division_names_group = 
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					motorized = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					motorized = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					motorized = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Armored Spearhead"
				#division_names_group = 
				priority = 2
				regiments = {
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					light_armor = { x = 0 y = 2 }

					owner = ROOT

					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 3\" division_template = \"Command Group\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 4\" division_template = \"Motorized Support Unit\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Boy 5\" division_template = \"Motorized Support Unit\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.8"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {

	title = stagpal.92.t
	desc = stagpal.92.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = stagpal.92.a
		add_popularity = {
    		ideology = democratic
    		popularity = 0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "LLama King"
				desc = "LLama_King_DESC"
				picture = ""
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = alicornrule
				traits = {
					SPL_King_of_the_LLamas
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = religios_pacifism
		swap_ruler_traits = { 
			remove = SPL_King_of_the_LLamas
			add = SPL_bishop_of_the_LLamas 
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_Goverment_was_overtaken
			add_idea = SPL_Goverment_became_religious
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = stagpal.102
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal.102"}
	title = stagpal.102.t
	desc = stagpal.102.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # an Alliance with friends
		name = stagpal.102.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = TIB
					is_in_faction_with = TIB
				}
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = stagpal.103 } #days to hours
		}
		TIB = {
			IF = {
				LIMIT = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}	
				create_faction = AIL_TIB_LLAMA_alliance
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				country_event = { id = stagpal.104 }#days to hours 
			}	
		}
	}
}

### Metal Raiders # To Do , Adds Reseach Bonus for light and Medium Tanks, as well as a tank IDea # And Descisions to make Hunter tanks , also for Artilery tanks, same with "Tank Plan"
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_military.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_military.9"}
	title = stagpal_military.9.t
	desc = stagpal_military.9.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # FASTER
		name = stagpal_military.9.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = gwtank
			}	
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = light_tank_equipment
				amount = 1000
				producer = SPL
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_light_tank_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = cat_light_armor
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Light_Tank_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 2
				category = cat_light_armor
			}
			Else = {
				set_technology = {
					gwtank = 1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = light_tank_equipment
					amount = 1000
					producer = SPL
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_light_tank_bonus
					bonus = 1.0
					uses = 1
					category = cat_light_armor
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_Light_Tank_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 2
					uses = 1
					category = cat_light_armor
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = basic_medium_tank
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_tank_equipment
				amount = 680
				producer = SPL
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_medium_tank_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = cat_medium_armor
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Medium_Tank_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 2
				category = cat_medium_armor
			}
			Else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_medium_tank_bonus
					bonus = 1.0
					uses = 1
					category = cat_medium_armor
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_Medium_Tank_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 2
					uses = 1
					category = cat_medium_armor
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SPL_Deer_Tank_focus_done # For the Descisions
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_idea = SPL_Metal_Raider_bonus_artillery
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SPL_Metal_Raider_bonus_artillery
				add_idea = SPL_Metal_Raider_bonus_artillery_and_tank
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = {
					SPL_Metal_Raider_bonus_tank
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Tank Plan # To Do , Adds Reseach Bonus for Heavy and Super Heavy Tanks, as well as a tank IDea # And Descisions to make Anti-Air tanks , also for Artilery tanks, same with "Metal Raiders"
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_military.20
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_military.20"}
	title = stagpal_military.20.t
	desc = stagpal_military.20.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Stronger
		name = stagpal_military.20.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = basic_heavy_tank
			}	
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = heavy_tank_equipment
				amount = 250
			#	producer = ROOT # To Do, Naming does nt show up perfectly , minor problem
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Heavy_tank_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = cat_heavy_armor
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Heavy_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 1
				category = cat_heavy_armor
			}
			Else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_Heavy_tank_bonus
					bonus = 1.25
					uses = 1
					category = cat_heavy_armor
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_HEAVY_Tank_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 3
					uses = 1
					category = cat_heavy_armor
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = super_heavy_tank
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = super_heavy_tank_equipment
				amount = 100
			#	producer = ROOT # To Do, Naming does nt show up perfectly , minor problem
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_SUPER_HEAVY_tank_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				technology = super_heavy_tank
				technology = super_heavy_tank_a 
				technology = super_heavy_tank_b	
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_SUPER_HEAVY_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 1
				technology = super_heavy_tank
				technology = super_heavy_tank_a 
				technology = super_heavy_tank_b	
			}
			Else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_SUPER_HEAVY_tank_bonus
					bonus = 1.25
					uses = 1
					technology = super_heavy_tank
					technology = super_heavy_tank_a 
					technology = super_heavy_tank_b	
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_SUPER_HEAVY_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 2
					uses = 1
					technology = super_heavy_tank
					technology = super_heavy_tank_a 
					technology = super_heavy_tank_b	
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SPL_LLama_Tank_focus_done # For the Descisions
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Tank_Plan_bonus_1
		}
	}
}

### Break Incoming threats # To Do , Adds Reseach Bonus for Anti-air and anti-tank, as well as a  IDea # And Descisions? maybe?
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_military.21
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_military.21"}
	title = stagpal_military.21.t
	desc = stagpal_military.21.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Just come to us
		name = stagpal_military.21.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = interwar_antiair
			}	
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = anti_air_equipment
				amount = 120
			#	producer = ROOT # To Do, Naming does nt show up perfectly , minor problem
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Anti_air_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = motorized_equipment
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Anti_air_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 1
				category = cat_anti_air
			}
			Else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_Anti_air_bonus
					bonus = 1.25
					uses = 1
					category = cat_anti_air
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_Anti_air_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 2
					uses = 1
					category = cat_anti_air
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = interwar_antitank 
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = anti_tank_equipment
				amount = 550
			#	producer = ROOT  # To Do, Naming does nt show up perfectly , minor problem
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_anti__tank_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = cat_anti_tank
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_anti_tank_ahead_bonus
				ahead_reduction = 2
				uses = 1
				category = cat_anti_tank
			}
			Else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_anti__tank_bonus
					bonus = 1.0
					uses = 1
					category = cat_anti_tank
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = SPL_anti_tank_ahead_bonus
					ahead_reduction = 2
					uses = 1
					category = cat_anti_tank
				}
			}
		}

		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SPL_Tank_Plan_bonus_1

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = stagpal_military.22
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_military.22"}
	title = stagpal_military.22.t
	desc = stagpal_military.22.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

		name = stagpal_military.22.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = early_bomber
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = SPL_Fighter_AIR_Medium_Bomber_Heavy_BOnus
				bonus = 2.5
				uses = 1
				category = tactical_bomber
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = tac_bomber_equipment
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SPL_Fighter_AIR_Medium_Bomber_BOnus
			bonus = 1.5
			uses = 1
			category = tactical_bomber
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SPL_DESTRUCTION_AIR_DOCTORIN_BOnus
			bonus = 1.5
			uses = 3
			category = cat_operational_integrity
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SPL_LLAMA_Fight_the_Air_1
			add_idea = SPL_LLAMA_Fight_the_Air_2
		}
		set_technology = {
			SPL_Better_Tactical_bombers_hidden = 1 #  To Do, Here we could maybe do some decision workprojects, must think for later
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = stagpal_news.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_news.1"}
	title = stagpal_news.1.t
	desc = stagpal_news.1.d
	
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = AIL
			NOT = {
				tag = AIL
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.b
		trigger = { 
 			tag = AIL 
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = AIL
					tag = AIL 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Young LLama Socialist"
			desc = "Young_LLama_Socialist_DESC"
			picture = ""
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
			traits = {
				SPL_young_llama_leader_trait
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = {
				SPL_Praesident_new_Llama
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # we gt them soon enough
		name = stagpal_oligarchie.3.h
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
				has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
				has_idea = SPL_Praesident_new_Deer
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {

			expire = "1965.1.1"

### The Idea of a King (Old Deer) / Factories to hord (Young Deer) / What they can't see (Old LLama) / Education, Exercise and fun (Young LLama)  ###  
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_oligarchie.15
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_oligarchie.15"}
	title = {
		text = stagpal_oligarchie.15.t.old_deers
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = stagpal_oligarchie.15.t.young_deers
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = stagpal_oligarchie.15.t.old_llama
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = stagpal_oligarchie.15.t.young_llamas
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = 	stagpal_oligarchie.15.d.old_llamas
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = 	stagpal_oligarchie.15.d.young_llamas
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = 	stagpal_oligarchie.15.d.old_deers
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = 	stagpal_oligarchie.15.d.young_deers
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
		}
	}
	
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # They will surely soon see it # Old Deer # To Do, maybe. I think A variable for king suppoert, or even depper game mechani cscould be fun. For now, jus a idea.
		name = stagpal_oligarchie.15.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_deers
		}
		add_political_power = -15
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Oligarchy_ideas_idea_of_a_King
		}
	}

	option = { # Factories to herd # Young Deer
		name = stagpal_oligarchie.15.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_deers
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Oligarchy_ideas_Factories_to_herd
		}		
	}

	option = { # They dont know that hit them # Old Llama # 
		name = stagpal_oligarchie.15.c
		add_political_power = 25
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_old_llamas
		}
		IF = {
			
			LIMIT = {
				has_dlc = "La Resistance"
			}
			IF = {
				LIMIT = {
					has_intelligence_agency = no
				}
				create_intelligence_agency = yes # creates with historical ones, if exists. 
				create_intelligence_agency = { 
 					 name = "What?" 
 					 icon = "GFX_intelligence_agency_logo_ita" 
				}
			}
			add_ideas = {
				SPL_Oligarchy_ideas_what_they_can_not_see
			}
			ELSE = {
				add_ideas = {
					SPL_Oligarchy_ideas_what_they_can_not_see_no_dlc
				}
			}	
		}
	}

	option = { # EEF makes us YEEF  # Young LLama
		name = stagpal_oligarchie.15.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPL_new_llamas
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 1
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			SPL_Oligarchy_ideas_Education_exercise_fun
		}
	}
}

### Mountain Farms experience ###
country_event = {
	id = Stagpal_Economics.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Stagpal_Economics.0"}
	title = Stagpal_Economics.0.t
	desc = Stagpal_Economics.0.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # A great experiance 
		name = Stagpal_Economics.0.a
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SPL_Mountain_farms_bonus
			bonus = 0.75
			uses = 1
			category = industry
		}
	}
}

### Mountain factories ###
country_event = {
	id = Stagpal_Economics.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Stagpal_Economics.1"}
	title = Stagpal_Economics.1.t
	desc = Stagpal_Economics.1.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # On the mountain we work
		name = Stagpal_Economics.1.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 1
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SPL_Mountain_factories_bonus
			bonus = 0.50
			uses = 1
			category = industry
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = Stagpal_Economics.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event Stagpal_Economics.2"}
	title = Stagpal_Economics.2.t
	desc = Stagpal_Economics.2.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Would be a Shame not to enrich ourselve
		name = Stagpal_Economics.2.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = synthetic_refinery
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = synthetic_refinery
									size > 1
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = synthetic_refinery 
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

### Inviting to a new Wolrd of fun and games # To Do, rather to look again. Might not work. Alis, EACH country that initially joins should add 4 Militray Factories
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_neffe.21
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_neffe.21"}
	title = stagpal_neffe.21.t
	desc = stagpal_neffe.21.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Yes , It is a wise choice
		name = stagpal_neffe.21.a
		FROM = {
			every_country = {
				LIMIT = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = THIS
						is_in_faction_with = THIS
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = FROM
			}
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = THIS
			country_event = { id = stagpal_neffe.22 } #days to hours apllied
		}
	}

	option = { # No, we don't want it
		name = stagpal_neffe.21.a
		every_neighbor_country = {
			country_event = { id = stagpal_neffe.23 } #days to hours apllied
		}
	}
}

### Schoolhouse Project
country_event = {
	id = stagpal_neffe.26
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_neffe.26"}
	title = stagpal_neffe.26.t
	desc = stagpal_neffe.26.d
		
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Kidz 
		name = stagpal_neffe.26.a
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = SPL_Neffe_techbonus_Intelligenz_Schoolhaus_project
			bonus = 0.5
    		uses = 1
			category = industry
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = stagpal_neffe.36.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_minority_rule
			add_idea = SPL_minority_rule_reduction_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea  = SPL_elitist_army
			add_idea = SPL_elitist_army_reduction_1
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}

# News Event
############

### Stagpal joins a faction ###
news_event = {
	id = stagpal_news.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_news.0"}
	title = stagpal_news.0.t
	desc = stagpal_news.0.d
	
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.0.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = AIL
			NOT = {
				tag = AIL
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.0.b
		trigger = { 
 			tag = AIL 
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.0.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = AIL
					tag = AIL 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### The LLama Faction ###
news_event = {
	id = stagpal_news.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event stagpal_news.1"}
	title = stagpal_news.1.t
	desc = stagpal_news.1.d
	
	#picture = GFX_event_lake_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = AIL
			NOT = {
				tag = AIL
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.b
		trigger = { 
 			tag = AIL 
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
	}
	option = {
		name = stagpal_news.1.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = AIL
					tag = AIL 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
